Fragment shader: ../p8/shader.frag
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 450 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in TESE_OUT {
 13 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 14 |	vec3 eyeDir;
 15 |    vec3 lightDir;
 16 |	vec3 worCord;
 17 |	vec3 eyeCord;
 18 |} from_tese;
 19 |
 20 |in float height;
 21 |
 22 |uniform	sampler2D texUnitHeightMap;
 23 |uniform	sampler2D normalMap;
 24 |uniform sampler1D colorGradient;
 25 |
 26 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 27 |//uniform vec3 light_pos = vec3(0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
 28 |//uniform vec3 light_pos;
 29 |//uniform vec4 fogColor = vec4(0.7, 0.7, 0.7, 1.0);
 30 |uniform bool useFog;
 31 |uniform bool useLight;
 32 |uniform int PP;
 33 |
 34 |out vec4 finalColor;
 35 |
 36 |vec4 mist(vec4 color)
 37 |{
 38 |	float z = length(from_tese.eyeCord);
 39 |	float de = 0.025*smoothstep(0.0,6.0,10.0-from_tese.worCord.y);
 40 |	float di = 0.045*smoothstep(0.0,40.0,20.0-from_tese.worCord.y);
 41 |	float forceExtinct = exp(-z*de);//absorb light
 42 |	float forceInscatt = exp(-z*di);//emit light
 43 |	return color*forceExtinct+fogColor*(1.0-forceInscatt);
 44 |}
 45 |
 46 |vec3 lightAndShadow ()
 47 |{
 48 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 49 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 50 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 51 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 52 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 53 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 54 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 55 |	recturn diff+spec;
 56 |}
 57 |
 58 |void main()
 59 |{
 60 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 61 |	switch(int(swapColor))
 62 |	{
 63 |		case 0:
 64 |		break;
 65 |		case 1:
 66 |			landColor = mist(landColor);
 67 |		break;
 68 |		case 2:
 69 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(),landColor.w);
 70 |		break;
 71 |		case 3:
 72 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(),landColor.w);
 73 |		break;
 74 |		default:
 75 |		break;
 76 |	};
 77 |	finalColor = landColor;
 78 |	/*
 79 |//=======================basic
 80 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 81 |	//=================================mist
 82 |	if (useFog)
 83 |	{
 84 |		landColor = mist(landColor);
 85 |	}
 86 |	//=========================light
 87 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 88 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 89 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 90 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 91 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 92 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 93 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 94 |	if (useLight)
 95 |	{
 96 |		landColor = vec4(diff+spec,landColor.w);
 97 |	}
 98 |	finalColor = landColor;
 99 |	*/
100 |}

Fragment shader: ../p8/shader.frag
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 450 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in TESE_OUT {
 13 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 14 |	vec3 eyeDir;
 15 |    vec3 lightDir;
 16 |	vec3 worCord;
 17 |	vec3 eyeCord;
 18 |} from_tese;
 19 |
 20 |in float height;
 21 |
 22 |uniform	sampler2D texUnitHeightMap;
 23 |uniform	sampler2D normalMap;
 24 |uniform sampler1D colorGradient;
 25 |
 26 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 27 |//uniform vec3 light_pos = vec3(0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
 28 |//uniform vec3 light_pos;
 29 |//uniform vec4 fogColor = vec4(0.7, 0.7, 0.7, 1.0);
 30 |uniform bool useFog;
 31 |uniform bool useLight;
 32 |uniform int PP;
 33 |
 34 |out vec4 finalColor;
 35 |
 36 |vec4 mist(vec4 color)
 37 |{
 38 |	float z = length(from_tese.eyeCord);
 39 |	float de = 0.025*smoothstep(0.0,6.0,10.0-from_tese.worCord.y);
 40 |	float di = 0.045*smoothstep(0.0,40.0,20.0-from_tese.worCord.y);
 41 |	float forceExtinct = exp(-z*de);//absorb light
 42 |	float forceInscatt = exp(-z*di);//emit light
 43 |	return color*forceExtinct+fogColor*(1.0-forceInscatt);
 44 |}
 45 |
 46 |vec3 lightAndShadow ()
 47 |{
 48 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 49 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 50 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 51 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 52 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 53 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 54 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 55 |	recturn diff+spec;
 56 |}
 57 |
 58 |void main()
 59 |{
 60 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 61 |	switch(int(PP))
 62 |	{
 63 |		case 0:
 64 |		break;
 65 |		case 1:
 66 |			landColor = mist(landColor);
 67 |		break;
 68 |		case 2:
 69 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(),landColor.w);
 70 |		break;
 71 |		case 3:
 72 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(),landColor.w);
 73 |		break;
 74 |		default:
 75 |		break;
 76 |	};
 77 |	finalColor = landColor;
 78 |	/*
 79 |//=======================basic
 80 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 81 |	//=================================mist
 82 |	if (useFog)
 83 |	{
 84 |		landColor = mist(landColor);
 85 |	}
 86 |	//=========================light
 87 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 88 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 89 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 90 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 91 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 92 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 93 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 94 |	if (useLight)
 95 |	{
 96 |		landColor = vec4(diff+spec,landColor.w);
 97 |	}
 98 |	finalColor = landColor;
 99 |	*/
100 |}

Fragment shader: ../p8/shader.frag

  1 |#version 450 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in TESE_OUT {
 13 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 14 |	vec3 eyeDir;
 15 |    vec3 lightDir;
 16 |	vec3 worCord;
 17 |	vec3 eyeCord;
 18 |} from_tese;
 19 |
 20 |in float height;
 21 |
 22 |uniform	sampler2D texUnitHeightMap;
 23 |uniform	sampler2D normalMap;
 24 |uniform sampler1D colorGradient;
 25 |
 26 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 27 |//uniform vec3 light_pos = vec3(0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
 28 |//uniform vec3 light_pos;
 29 |uniform vec4 fogColor = vec4(0.7, 0.7, 0.7, 1.0);
 30 |uniform bool useFog;
 31 |uniform bool useLight;
 32 |uniform int PP;
 33 |
 34 |out vec4 finalColor;
 35 |
 36 |vec4 mist(vec4 color)
 37 |{
 38 |	float z = length(from_tese.eyeCord);
 39 |	float de = 0.025*smoothstep(0.0,6.0,10.0-from_tese.worCord.y);
 40 |	float di = 0.045*smoothstep(0.0,40.0,20.0-from_tese.worCord.y);
 41 |	float forceExtinct = exp(-z*de);//absorb light
 42 |	float forceInscatt = exp(-z*di);//emit light
 43 |	return color*forceExtinct+fogColor*(1.0-forceInscatt);
 44 |}
 45 |
 46 |vec3 lightAndShadow (vec4 landColor)
 47 |{
 48 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 49 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 50 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 51 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 52 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 53 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 54 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 55 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 56 |	return diff+spec;
 57 |}
 58 |
 59 |void main()
 60 |{
 61 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 62 |	switch(int(PP))
 63 |	{
 64 |		case 0:
 65 |		break;
 66 |		case 1:
 67 |			landColor = mist(landColor);
 68 |		break;
 69 |		case 2:
 70 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(landColor),landColor.w);
 71 |		break;
 72 |		case 3:
 73 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(landColor),landColor.w);
 74 |		break;
 75 |		default:
 76 |		break;
 77 |	};
 78 |	finalColor = landColor;
 79 |	/*
 80 |//=======================basic
 81 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 82 |	//=================================mist
 83 |	if (useFog)
 84 |	{
 85 |		landColor = mist(landColor);
 86 |	}
 87 |	//=========================light
 88 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 89 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 90 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 91 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 92 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 93 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 94 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 95 |	if (useLight)
 96 |	{
 97 |		landColor = vec4(diff+spec,landColor.w);
 98 |	}
 99 |	finalColor = landColor;
100 |	*/
101 |}

Tessellation evaluation shader: ../p8/shader.tese
-------------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 450 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (quads, equal_spacing, ccw) in;
  4 |
  5 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  6 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  9 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
 10 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
 11 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 12 |};
 13 |
 14 |uniform	sampler2D texUnitHeightMap;
 15 |uniform float depth;
 16 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 17 |uniform vec3 light_pos = vec3(0.0, 100.0, 100.00);
 18 |uniform int PP;
 19 |uniform vec3 lightDirUI;
 20 |
 21 |in TESC_OUT {
 22 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 23 |} from_tesc[];
 24 |
 25 |out TESE_OUT {
 26 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 27 |	vec3 eyeDir;//reserved for tangens
 28 |    vec3 lightDir;//tangent light
 29 |	vec3 worCord;
 30 |	vec3 eyeCord;
 31 |} from_tese;
 32 |
 33 |out float height;
 34 |
 35 |void main()
 36 |{
 37 |	vec2 t1 = mix(from_tesc[0].textureCoord, from_tesc[1].textureCoord, gl_TessCoord.x);
 38 |	vec2 t2 = mix(from_tesc[2].textureCoord, from_tesc[3].textureCoord, gl_TessCoord.x);
 39 |
 40 |	from_tese.textureCoord = mix(t2, t1, gl_TessCoord.y);
 41 |
 42 |	vec4 p1 = mix(gl_in[0].gl_Position, gl_in[1].gl_Position, gl_TessCoord.x);
 43 |	vec4 p2 = mix(gl_in[2].gl_Position, gl_in[3].gl_Position, gl_TessCoord.x);
 44 |
 45 |	vec4 p = mix(p2, p1, gl_TessCoord.y);
 46 |	height = texture(texUnitHeightMap, from_tese.textureCoord).x;
 47 |	p.y += height * depth;
 48 |
 49 |	//vec4 p01 = gl_in[0].gl_Position;
 50 |	//vec4 p02 = gl_in[1].gl_Position;
 51 |	//vec4 p03 = gl_in[2].gl_Position;
 52 |	//vec3 v1 = normalize(p02.xyz - p01.xyz);
 53 |	//vec3 v2 = normalize(p03.xyz - p01.xyz);
 54 |
 55 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * p;
 56 |	//============================================mist
 57 |	vec4 eyeP = modelviewMatrix * p;
 58 |	from_tese.worCord = p.xyz;
 59 |	from_tese.eyeCord = eyeP.xyz;
 60 |	//============================================light
 61 |	vec4 P = modelviewMatrix * p;
 62 |	switch(int(PP))
 63 |	{
 64 |		case 0:
 65 |			vec4 light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 66 |		break;
 67 |		case 1:
 68 |			vec4 light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 69 |		break;
 70 |		case 2:
 71 |			vec4 light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 72 |		break;
 73 |		case 3:
 74 |			vec4 light = viewMatrix*vec4(lightDirUI,1.0);
 75 |		break;
 76 |		default:
 77 |			vec4 light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 78 |		break;
 79 |	};
 80 |	vec3 normal = vec3(0.0,1.0,0.0);
 81 |	vec3 tangent = vec3(1.0,0.0,0.0);
 82 |	vec3 N = normalize(mat3(modelviewMatrix)*normal);
 83 |	vec3 T = normalize(mat3(modelviewMatrix)*tangent);
 84 |	vec3 B = cross(N, T);
 85 |	//mat3 TBN = mat3(T, B, N);
 86 |	vec3 L = light.xyz - P.xyz;
 87 |	from_tese.lightDir = normalize(vec3(dot(L,T),dot(L,B),dot(L,N)));
 88 |	vec3 V = -P.xyz;
 89 |	from_tese.eyeDir = normalize(vec3(dot(V,T),dot(V,B),dot(V,N)));
 90 |}
 91 |

 23 |} from_tesc[];

Tessellation evaluation shader: ../p8/shader.tese
-------------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 450 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (quads, equal_spacing, ccw) in;
  4 |
  5 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  6 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  9 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
 10 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
 11 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 12 |};
 13 |
 14 |uniform	sampler2D texUnitHeightMap;
 15 |uniform float depth;
 16 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 17 |uniform vec3 light_pos = vec3(0.0, 100.0, 100.00);
 18 |uniform int PP;
 19 |uniform vec3 lightDirUI;
 20 |
 21 |in TESC_OUT {
 22 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 23 |} from_tesc[];
 24 |
 25 |out TESE_OUT {
 26 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 27 |	vec3 eyeDir;//reserved for tangens
 28 |    vec3 lightDir;//tangent light
 29 |	vec3 worCord;
 30 |	vec3 eyeCord;
 31 |} from_tese;
 32 |
 33 |out float height;
 34 |
 35 |void main()
 36 |{
 37 |	vec2 t1 = mix(from_tesc[0].textureCoord, from_tesc[1].textureCoord, gl_TessCoord.x);
 38 |	vec2 t2 = mix(from_tesc[2].textureCoord, from_tesc[3].textureCoord, gl_TessCoord.x);
 39 |
 40 |	from_tese.textureCoord = mix(t2, t1, gl_TessCoord.y);
 41 |
 42 |	vec4 p1 = mix(gl_in[0].gl_Position, gl_in[1].gl_Position, gl_TessCoord.x);
 43 |	vec4 p2 = mix(gl_in[2].gl_Position, gl_in[3].gl_Position, gl_TessCoord.x);
 44 |
 45 |	vec4 p = mix(p2, p1, gl_TessCoord.y);
 46 |	height = texture(texUnitHeightMap, from_tese.textureCoord).x;
 47 |	p.y += height * depth;
 48 |
 49 |	//vec4 p01 = gl_in[0].gl_Position;
 50 |	//vec4 p02 = gl_in[1].gl_Position;
 51 |	//vec4 p03 = gl_in[2].gl_Position;
 52 |	//vec3 v1 = normalize(p02.xyz - p01.xyz);
 53 |	//vec3 v2 = normalize(p03.xyz - p01.xyz);
 54 |
 55 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * p;
 56 |	//============================================mist
 57 |	vec4 eyeP = modelviewMatrix * p;
 58 |	from_tese.worCord = p.xyz;
 59 |	from_tese.eyeCord = eyeP.xyz;
 60 |	//============================================light
 61 |	vec4 P = modelviewMatrix * p;
 62 |	vec4 light = vec4*=(0.0f);
 63 |	switch(int(PP))
 64 |	{
 65 |		case 0:
 66 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 67 |		break;
 68 |		case 1:
 69 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 70 |		break;
 71 |		case 2:
 72 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 73 |		break;
 74 |		case 3:
 75 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(lightDirUI,1.0);
 76 |		break;
 77 |		default:
 78 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 79 |		break;
 80 |	};
 81 |	vec3 normal = vec3(0.0,1.0,0.0);
 82 |	vec3 tangent = vec3(1.0,0.0,0.0);
 83 |	vec3 N = normalize(mat3(modelviewMatrix)*normal);
 84 |	vec3 T = normalize(mat3(modelviewMatrix)*tangent);
 85 |	vec3 B = cross(N, T);
 86 |	//mat3 TBN = mat3(T, B, N);
 87 |	vec3 L = light.xyz - P.xyz;
 88 |	from_tese.lightDir = normalize(vec3(dot(L,T),dot(L,B),dot(L,N)));
 89 |	vec3 V = -P.xyz;
 90 |	from_tese.eyeDir = normalize(vec3(dot(V,T),dot(V,B),dot(V,N)));
 91 |}
 92 |

 35 |void main()
 36 |{
 37 |	vec2 t1 = mix(from_tesc[0].textureCoord, from_tesc[1].textureCoord, gl_TessCoord.x);
 38 |	vec2 t2 = mix(from_tesc[2].textureCoord, from_tesc[3].textureCoord, gl_TessCoord.x);
 39 |
 40 |	from_tese.textureCoord = mix(t2, t1, gl_TessCoord.y);
 41 |
 42 |	vec4 p1 = mix(gl_in[0].gl_Position, gl_in[1].gl_Position, gl_TessCoord.x);
 43 |	vec4 p2 = mix(gl_in[2].gl_Position, gl_in[3].gl_Position, gl_TessCoord.x);
 44 |
 45 |	vec4 p = mix(p2, p1, gl_TessCoord.y);
 46 |	height = texture(texUnitHeightMap, from_tese.textureCoord).x;
 47 |	p.y += height * depth;
 48 |
 49 |	//vec4 p01 = gl_in[0].gl_Position;
 50 |	//vec4 p02 = gl_in[1].gl_Position;
 51 |	//vec4 p03 = gl_in[2].gl_Position;
 52 |	//vec3 v1 = normalize(p02.xyz - p01.xyz);
 53 |	//vec3 v2 = normalize(p03.xyz - p01.xyz);
 54 |
 55 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * p;
 56 |	//============================================mist
 57 |	vec4 eyeP = modelviewMatrix * p;
 58 |	from_tese.worCord = p.xyz;
 59 |	from_tese.eyeCord = eyeP.xyz;
 60 |	//============================================light
 61 |	vec4 P = modelviewMatrix * p;
 62 |	vec4 light = vec4*(0.0f);
 63 |	
 64 |	switch(int(PP))
 65 |	{
 66 |		case 0:
 67 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 68 |		break;
 69 |		case 1:
 70 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 71 |		break;
 72 |		case 2:
 73 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 74 |		break;
 75 |		case 3:
 76 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(lightDirUI,1.0);
 77 |		break;
 78 |		default:
 79 |			light = viewMatrix*vec4(light_pos,1.0);
 80 |		break;
 81 |	};
 82 |	vec3 normal = vec3(0.0,1.0,0.0);
 83 |	vec3 tangent = vec3(1.0,0.0,0.0);
 84 |	vec3 N = normalize(mat3(modelviewMatrix)*normal);
 85 |	vec3 T = normalize(mat3(modelviewMatrix)*tangent);
 86 |	vec3 B = cross(N, T);
 87 |	//mat3 TBN = mat3(T, B, N);
 88 |	vec3 L = light.xyz - P.xyz;
 89 |	from_tese.lightDir = normalize(vec3(dot(L,T),dot(L,B),dot(L,N)));
 90 |	vec3 V = -P.xyz;
 91 |	from_tese.eyeDir = normalize(vec3(dot(V,T),dot(V,B),dot(V,N)));
 92 |}

Fragment shader: ../p8/shader.frag
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 450 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in TESE_OUT {
 13 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 14 |	vec3 eyeDir;
 15 |    vec3 lightDir;
 16 |	vec3 worCord;
 17 |	vec3 eyeCord;
 18 |} from_tese;
 19 |
 20 |in float height;
 21 |
 22 |uniform	sampler2D texUnitHeightMap;
 23 |uniform	sampler2D normalMap;
 24 |uniform sampler1D colorGradient;
 25 |
 26 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 27 |//uniform vec3 light_pos = vec3(0.0, 100.0, 100.0);
 28 |//uniform vec3 light_pos;
 29 |uniform vec4 fogColor = vec4(0.7, 0.7, 0.7, 1.0);
 30 |uniform bool useFog;
 31 |uniform bool useLight;
 32 |uniform int PP;
 33 |uniform vec3 lightDirUI;
 34 |uniform float eat, eati, emit, emiti;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 finalColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec4 mist(vec4 color)
 39 |{
 40 |	float z = length(from_tese.eyeCord);
 41 |	float de = eati*smoothstep(0.0,eat,eat*2-from_tese.worCord.y);
 42 |	float di = emiti*smoothstep(0.0,emit,emit/2-from_tese.worCord.y);
 43 |	float forceExtinct = exp(-z*de);//absorb light
 44 |	float forceInscatt = exp(-z*di);//emit light
 45 |	return color*forceExtinct+fogColor*(1.0-forceInscatt);
 46 |}
 47 |
 48 |vec3 lightAndShadow (vec3 landColor)
 49 |{
 50 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
 51 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 52 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 53 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
 54 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
 55 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
 56 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
 57 |	return diff+spec;
 58 |}
 59 |
 60 |vec3 lightAndShadow2(vec3 landColor)
 61 |{
 62 |vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
 63 |    int directCheck = 1;
 64 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
 65 |    float aten = 1;
 66 |
 67 |    vec3 L_nagative = -L;
 68 |    float foco = 1.0;
 69 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 70 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 71 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 72 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 73 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 74 |	  shininess=2;
 75 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 76 |    }
 77 |
 78 |    color += aten * foco * (
 79 |             landColor * diffuseMult +
 80 |             specularMult);
 81 |  }
 82 |
 83 |  return color;
 84 |  }
 85 |
 86 |void main()
 87 |{
 88 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
 89 |	switch(int(PP))
 90 |	{
 91 |		case 0:
 92 |		break;
 93 |		case 1:
 94 |			landColor = mist(landColor);
 95 |		break;
 96 |		case 2:
 97 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(landColor.xyz),landColor.w);
 98 |		break;
 99 |		case 3:
100 |			landColor = vec4(lightAndShadow(landColor.xyz),landColor.w);
101 |		break;
102 |		default:
103 |		break;
104 |	};
105 |	finalColor = landColor;
106 |	/*
107 |//=======================basic
108 |	vec4 landColor = texture(colorGradient, height);
109 |	//=================================mist
110 |	if (useFog)
111 |	{
112 |		landColor = mist(landColor);
113 |	}
114 |	//=========================light
115 |    vec3 V = normalize(from_tese.eyeDir);
116 |    vec3 L = normalize(from_tese.lightDir);
117 |    vec3 N = normalize(texture(normalMap, from_tese.textureCoord).rgb*2.0f - vec3(1.0f));
118 |	vec3 R = reflect(-L,N);
119 |	vec3 diff = max(dot(N,L),0.0)*landColor.xyz;
120 |	vec3 specShine = vec3(0.1);
121 |	vec3 spec = max(pow(dot(R,V),5.0),0.0)*specShine;
122 |	if (useLight)
123 |	{
124 |		landColor = vec4(diff+spec,landColor.w);
125 |	}
126 |	finalColor = landColor;
127 |	*/
128 |}
129 |
